{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"IKEA inspires us to repurpose 12 products, including this greenhouse","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=83743","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p class=\"has-medium-font-size\"><em>Repurposeful Instructions for an IKEA cabinet that begs to be a greenhouse.</em></p> <p>IKEA seems to have caught the hacking (or repurposing) bug. Just last week, I featured IKEA Netherlands inviting <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/08/circular-hub-ikea.html\">12 artists to shop the As-Is</a> (Circular Hub, nowadays) and turn the items into works of art.</p> <p>Now <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/ca/en/campaigns/one-little-thing-pub91090cf0#6234d690-ee26-11eb-b28d-83bc1a39a29f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA Canada</a> gives us another set of exciting repurposed IKEA items. I can only assume more and more IKEA locations will start sharing their modifications, as the company moves towards being fully circular by 2030. </p> <p>Our Canadian IKEA co-workers have created 12 IKEA repurposeful instructions, ranging from beginner to advanced projects. All accessible from <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/ca/en/campaigns/one-little-thing-pub91090cf0#6234d690-ee26-11eb-b28d-83bc1a39a29f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">this page</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1108\" height=\"622\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-canada-repurposeful-instructions-2.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA Repurposeful Instructions\" class=\"wp-image-83747\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-canada-repurposeful-instructions-2.jpg 1108w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-canada-repurposeful-instructions-2-550x309.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-canada-repurposeful-instructions-2-768x431.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1108px) 100vw, 1108px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>IKEA Repurposeful Instructions: Beginners</h5> <p>The Beginner’s projects focus on repurposing items, such as the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/variera-plastic-bag-dispenser-white-80010222/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">VARIERA plastic bag dispenser</a> into a cleaning caddy. That IKEA item is — for sure — a handy one. On IKEAhackers, we’ve also turned them into a <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2012/05/yarnbombing-station.html\">Yarn Station</a>, <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2019/11/ikea-gift-wrap-storage-ideas.html\">Gift Wrap holder</a>, even a low <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2011/10/low-budget-bedside-lamp.html\">budget bedside lamp</a>.</p> <p>Other projects include a candle holder repurposed into a planter, art display, toys storage and organizers.</p> <p class=\"has-text-align-left\">I also like the FABRIKÖR terrarium, very much in line with the <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/ikeagreenhousecabinet/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA greenhouse cabinet</a> trend. </p> <p>For this project, you’ll need the \n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   FABRIKÖR cabinet, plants and weather stripping. They recommend a humidity monitor too.\n  </meta></p> <p>According to their instructions, drawn in the IKEA assembly manual style, you’ll need to apply <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3fXfToD\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">weather stripping</a> to the interior seams of the cabinet to create a moisture seal. Then, add the plants and you’re done! </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-medium\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"550\" height=\"801\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-fabrikor-greenhouse-1-550x801.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA Repurposeful Instructions - FABRIKOR greenhouse\" class=\"wp-image-83750\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-fabrikor-greenhouse-1-550x801.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-fabrikor-greenhouse-1.jpg 703w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 550px) 100vw, 550px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Personal experience tells me keeping a plant alive needs more than that. Installing some grow lights and fans may be necessary too. But, this is the basic version of a greenhouse. And it’s a good place to start.</p> <h5>Going intermediate</h5> <p>The Intermediate projects are a little more involved. </p> <p>Continuing with the green-theme, the FRAKTA hanging planter is a pretty one. You’ll need the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/frakta-shopping-bag-medium-blue-60301707/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">medium sized blue bags</a>, rope and S-hooks. </p> <p>Check out the video below for a quick look at how the planter is done.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\">\n  <div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\"> \n   <iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"IKEA Repurposeful Instructions | FRAKTA GARDEN\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/030ab0GcO2Q?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe> \n  </div>\n </figure> <p>Looks familiar? You bet. Way back in 2014, we featured the <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2014/03/hanging-gardens.html\">hanging bag planter hack</a> below with smaller custom sewn IKEA bags and metal chains (much easier to reposition). Now, you can omit the sewing with the smallest blue bag, <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/brattby-bag-blue-20103648/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">BRATTBY</a>. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/rsz_balkonampel.jpg\" alt=\"hanging blue bag planter\" width=\"600\" height=\"900\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Included in this Intermediate section is a RIBBA organizer and ASXTAD shoe drawer. </p> <h5>Advanced projects</h5> <p>The last category is where you’ll need to bring out the power tools. </p> <p>The two projects are for birds and bees.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-repurposeful-instructions.png\" alt=\"IKEA repurposeful instructions\" class=\"wp-image-83744\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-repurposeful-instructions.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-repurposeful-instructions-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-repurposeful-instructions-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>The first is an IVAR beehive with room for 24 hives. </p> <p>In a nutshell, the IVAR shelves are modified into brackets, attached to the interior side walls of the IVAR. There is enough room in the cabinet for 3 levels. The hives then hang from these brackets. </p> <p>The second project is a <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/06/ikea-socker-window-bird-feeder.html\">cute birdhouse</a> from BLANDA MATT wooden bowl. (Joining two bowls reminds me of this <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/05/stereo-system-with-4-bland-matt-bowls-and-2-lack-shelves.html\">sphere speaker hack</a>.) What I like most about it? The Allen Key perch. </p> <p>Visit <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/ca/en/campaigns/one-little-thing-pub91090cf0#6234d690-ee26-11eb-b28d-83bc1a39a29f\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA Canada to browse the manuals</a>. It’s worth a look.</p> <p>Have you attempted anything similar? If so let us know and <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/submit-hack\">share your ideas</a> too.</p> </span>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" Yap","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-canada-repurposeful-instructions-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn4@2020_4/2021/08/15/03-55-00-787_eeae3674c953239e.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-fabrikor-greenhouse-1-550x801.jpg":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/02/rsz_balkonampel.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn100@2020_3/2021/08/15/03-55-01-747_8721132536cff09d.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-repurposeful-instructions.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn92@2020_1/2021/08/15/03-55-01-806_0e678ffcffbe5e8e.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn32@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-02-316_05353866f732d1c2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn72@2020_3/2021/08/15/03-55-01-886_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=i6Mg_k2Smu0:iubZFRStHIM:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn71@2020_4/2021/08/15/03-55-01-698_3b855d375f262bbe.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/i6Mg_k2Smu0":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn31@2020_2/2021/08/15/03-55-02-019_02c4aa7a893f5e31.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1628999639625},{"createdTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"12 artists hack IKEA bargain items and we’re stoked!","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=83664","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>The As-Is or Bargain Corner is, hands down, our favourite spot in all of IKEA. </p> <p>In there, we find treasures like ex-showroom furniture, items without packaging, items that are out of the range or products with scratches or minor damage. Best thing, all at reduced prices. </p> <p>Perfect for hacking. In fact, we have a page full of <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?s=as-is\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">hacks made from As-Is items</a>.</p> <h3>Bargain Corner to Circular Hub</h3> <p>But things are always evolving. IKEA realised that it’s not merely about reduced prices. Rather, giving these items a second chance, extending their life cycle and reusing resources. The concept of circularity is to make it easier for customers to acquire, care for and pass on products in circular ways, such as repairing, reusing, reselling, and recycling them. </p> <p>So the humble Bargain Corner (or known as As-is corner, in some markets) is now rebranded as Circular Hub. It may not have changed at your local IKEA yet, but it will come. <a href=\"https://about.ikea.com/en/sustainability/a-world-without-waste/why-the-future-of-furniture-is-circular\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA hopes to be 100% circular by 2030</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"576\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1.jpeg\" alt=\"IKEA circular hub\" class=\"wp-image-83669\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1-550x309.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1-768x432.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> <p>To bring this concept to life, IKEA Netherlands invited 12 artists to shop the Circular Hub and turn them into works of art. Right up our alley.</p> <p>These are my favourites. <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/nl/campaigns/koopjeshoek-wordt-circular-hub-pub99000e50\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See all 12 here</a>.</p> <h3>Shine on flowers</h3> <p>Cedric used a&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/p/nymane-floor-lamp-white-60336759/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">NYMÅNE floor&nbsp;lamp</a>, lots of artificial flowers and a <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3ljz0Nl\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">glue gun</a> to create a whimsical “bouquet that lights up”. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/nymane-floor-lamp-hack.png\" alt=\"NYMANE lamp hack\" class=\"wp-image-83665\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/nymane-floor-lamp-hack.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/nymane-floor-lamp-hack-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/nymane-floor-lamp-hack-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">IKEA.nl</a></p> <h3>Knotted up</h3> <p>For her project, artist Loes used a&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/p/praestholm-bench-with-backrest-outdoor-grey-70418170/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">PRÄSTHOLM</a>&nbsp;outdoor sofa.</p> <p>She painted the grey metal and wood sofa in light pastel green. Then wrapped strands of paracord around the bars. The end result is a bright, cheerful, one-of-a-kind garden bench. Love how customizable this is with different coloured ropes and <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3xjeKO3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">knot patterns</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/prastholm-sofa-hack.png\" alt=\"Prastholm sofa hack - circular hub\" class=\"wp-image-83666\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/prastholm-sofa-hack.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/prastholm-sofa-hack-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/prastholm-sofa-hack-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">\n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   Photo: \n   <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">IKEA.nl</a>\n  </meta></p> <p> </p> <h3>Pieces of art</h3> <p>Her piece is definitely more involved. Tamar smashed up pieces of ceramics (tiles, cups, plates) and arranged them on the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/hemnes-glass-door-cabinet-white-stain-90371770/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">HEMNES&nbsp;display cabinet</a> until she got a design she was happy with. Then, glued each piece down. To set the “stones”, she filled all the joints with grout compound. Lastly, brushed away all the grout and glue traces with a damp sponge. And the cabinet becomes a display in itself.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-glass-cabinet-hack.png\" alt=\"HEMNES display cabinet - circular hub\" class=\"wp-image-83667\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-glass-cabinet-hack.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-glass-cabinet-hack-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-glass-cabinet-hack-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">\n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   Photo: \n   <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">IKEA.nl</a>\n  </meta></p> <h3>A shoe-in </h3> <p>Belen used a&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-with-2-compartments-white-20169559/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">HEMNES&nbsp;shoe&nbsp;cabinet</a> to put her stamp on. After cleaning the furniture with degreaser, she sanded it and applied a coat of chalk paint. Lastly she applied white wood glue and stuck the decoupage paper on it. Finished with a coat of <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2WKN4oR\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">furniture wax.</a> </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-hack.png\" alt=\"HEMNES shoe cabinet hack\" class=\"wp-image-83668\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-hack.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-hack-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-hack-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">\n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   Photo: \n   <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/nl/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">IKEA.nl</a>\n  </meta></p> <p>Which is your favourite? +0000","feedId":65,"bgimg":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1.jpeg","linkMd5":"9f39d609cf8e848a1153663ffc40174c","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn24@2020_4/2021/08/15/03-55-00-750_2dcdd06264667e94.webp","destWidth":1024,"destHeight":576,"sourceBytes":88761,"destBytes":57418,"author":"Jules Yap","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/IKEA_Still-circular-Hub_01-1024x576-1.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn24@2020_4/2021/08/15/03-55-00-750_2dcdd06264667e94.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/nymane-floor-lamp-hack.png":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/prastholm-sofa-hack.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn64@2020_2/2021/08/15/03-55-02-604_a764ca6d11b5f41c.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-glass-cabinet-hack.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn56@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-02-404_72022896ffbe8a0a.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/hemnes-shoe-cabinet-hack.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn28@2020_2/2021/08/15/03-55-01-711_a3e8f5fe7abcdfd8.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn32@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-02-316_05353866f732d1c2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn72@2020_3/2021/08/15/03-55-01-886_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=ZFH4D1GaWMc:sf8cOCrz4N4:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn68@2020_4/2021/08/15/03-55-01-694_0a655cc50fb8233f.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/ZFH4D1GaWMc":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn95@2020_3/2021/08/15/03-55-02-476_dc71d50f187899ff.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1628999639655},{"createdTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"6 money saving ideas to upcycle your old IKEA crib","link":"https://ikeahackers.net/?p=67128","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>Kids outgrown the IKEA crib? Reinvent it into another useful piece of furniture. The <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/sniglar-crib-beech-50248541/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">SNIGLAR</a> or <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/gulliver-crib-white-80248525/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">GULLIVER</a> is awesome in the laundry room, even in the kitchen and study.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"282\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ikea-crib-sniglar-gulliver-1.png\" alt=\"IKEA crib\" class=\"wp-image-83651\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ikea-crib-sniglar-gulliver-1.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ikea-crib-sniglar-gulliver-1-550x207.png 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">IKEA <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/sniglar-crib-beech-50248541/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">SNIGLAR</a> and <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/gulliver-crib-white-80248525/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">GULLIVER</a> crib | IKEA.com</p> <h5>3 ways to use IKEA SNIGLAR crib for laundry </h5> <p>Michal shares 3 wonderful ideas for an old unused IKEA SNIGLAR crib. The crib is repurposed to now hang the never ending heap of laundry. </p> <p>All 3 hacks are made from one SNIGLAR crib using the sidewalls only, original fasteners, additional screws, a piece of board and 4 caster wheels. </p> <p>You don’t not need much tools except for a <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3j23znN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">handsaw</a>, sand paper, and <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2UVo6Tf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">cordless drill</a>.</p> <h3>#1 Extension to ladder towel rail</h3> <p>The problem with ladder towel rails is that bathroom towels constantly fall down from the rail. And not many towels can be dried all at once. And what if you have other odd shaped washing to be dried? Here’s our solution.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter is-resized\">\n   <a href=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-heating-rail.jpg\"><img loading=\"lazy\" src=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-heating-rail-550x310.jpg\" alt=\"ladder towel rail extension hack\" width=\"550\" height=\"310\" /></a>\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>1. Measure the width of your <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3lc3CAf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">straight ladder towel rail warmer<img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1\" height=\"1\" border=\"0\" style=\"border: none !important; margin: 0px !important;\" src=\"https://ir-na.amazon-adsystem.com/e/ir?t=ikeahacker-20&amp;l=am2&amp;o=1&amp;a=B01HR4H770\" alt=\"\" /></a>.</p> <p>2. Cut the SNIGLAR bars to fit the width and slot it into the towel rail.</p> <p>3. The protruding bars serve as pegs for towels and other washing.</p> <h3>#2 Portable drying rack</h3> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n   <a href=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-portable-drying-rack.jpg\"><img src=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-portable-drying-rack-550x309.jpg\" alt=\"Portable drying rack from IKEA SNIGLAR crib\" /></a>\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>1. Cut one of the sidewalls of the crib and remove the top rail that hold the bars together.</p> <p>2. Cut the top rail into two equal pieces and make a notch in the middle.</p> <p>3. Fasten the sidewall cut in Step 1 onto the notched pieces.</p> <p>Just place this portable dryer in front of the fireplace&nbsp;or central heating system and let the clothes dry out.</p> <h3>#3 Large capacity laundry basket</h3> <p>Get rid of piles of dirty clothes lying around. With this hack you will build a robust basket that you can move with ease.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n   <a href=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-laundry-basket.jpg\"><img src=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Sniglar-laundry-basket-550x309.jpg\" alt=\"DIY large capacity laundry basket from IKEA SNIGLAR crib\" /></a>\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>1. Cut both the long sections of the sidewalls of the crib and the short sidewall. Remove the legs as well.</p> <p>2. Join them together using the original fasteners and additional screws where necessary.</p> <p>3. Get a board to create the base. We added extra length at the side and back to serve as wall protection.</p> <p>4. Screw the board into the sidewalls from under the board.</p> <p>5. Add casters.</p> <p>6. Staple firm fabric inside the cavity.</p> <p>7. Roll it into the space beside your washing machine.</p> <p>See how we hacked it. <a href=\"https://youtu.be/MB62fLyeqKw\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Link to video</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\">\n  <div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\"> \n   <iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"3 awesome IKEA hacks for laundry and drying in large family\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/MB62fLyeqKw?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe> \n  </div>\n </figure> <p>~ by Michal</p> <h3>#4 IKEA crib drying rack</h3> <p>This <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2014/10/gulliver-travels-to-the-laundry-room.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">wall mounted retractable laundry rack</a> will hold up a load of washing. Very useful if you have a small laundry area. You can use the IKEA GULLIVER or SNIGLAR crib for this purpose. Picture below shows the GULLIVER. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/20141005_140614.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA GULLIVER crib laundry rack\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Use straight mending plates to join the sidewalls together. You can use one section or two sections, depending on how tall a rack you need. But more than two is not recommended as the rack may get too heavy with a full load of laundry. Then attach the rack to the wall using two heavy duty hinges. Finish with a pulley and rope and a cleat hook to hold it in place. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2014/10/gulliver-travels-to-the-laundry-room.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See the full tutorial</a>. (<a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2016/06/singular-baby-cot-retractable-drying-rack.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">SNIGLAR version</a>.) </p> <h3>#5 Cookie drying rack</h3> <p>Need a drying rack for your baked goods? Much cheaper and easier to have IKEA make it. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2012/09/making-a-drying-rack.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Read more</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/blogger/-WJOAat2211o/UFhmdblPDaI/AAAAAAAArOI/Reh4kYw1ihs/s640/bedruktsnoep1-776462.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA crib drying rack\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h3>#6 Kids desk</h3> <p>The little one is ready to write and draw. Adjust the height of the cross bar by drilling mounting holes at appropriate height and turn the crib into a <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/category/hacks/children/desks-chairs\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">kids desk</a>. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/10/kids-artcrafthomework-table-from-ikea-gulliver-cot.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See details of the kids desk project</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"703\" height=\"942\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/IKEA-kids-side_1.jpg\" alt=\"kids desk hacked from cot\" class=\"wp-image-83652\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/IKEA-kids-side_1.jpg 703w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/IKEA-kids-side_1-550x737.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 703px) 100vw, 703px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h3>#7 Computer desk from old crib</h3> <p>The desk setup can work for adults too.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/computer-desk.jpg\" alt=\"computer desk hacked from IKEA GULLIVER crib\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Andrijana made a computer desk from her son’s old&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/gulliver\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA GULLIVER</a>&nbsp;crib. Add an IKEA LINNMON table on top and secure the table top to the crib frame with L-brackets. If you prefer more legroom, flip the crib over and place the table top on the “feet” of the GULLIVER instead. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2019/01/computer-desk-ikea-crib.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See the tutorial</a>.</p> <p class=\"has-small-font-size\"><em>First published on April 10, 2017. Updated with new content.</em></p> </span>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/07/ikea-crib-upcycle-ideas.html\">6 money saving ideas to upcycle your old IKEA 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"IKEA FALSTER garden set gets a facelift","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=83674","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>As you can see in the before picture, the faded brown was not looking good. I was debating on what to do as the IKEA FALSTER garden set is still in good shape on its own. </p> <p>I thought of painting it to see how it will look and I love the final look.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"449\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-3.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-3-550x241.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-3-768x337.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>IKEA items used: </h5> \n <ul>\n  <li>IKEA FALSTER outdoor dining set</li>\n </ul> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"688\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/ikea-falster-outdoor-dining-set.png\" alt=\"falster outdoor furniture\n\" class=\"wp-image-77631\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/ikea-falster-outdoor-dining-set.png 1000w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/ikea-falster-outdoor-dining-set-550x378.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/ikea-falster-outdoor-dining-set-768x528.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>Other Materials and Tools: </h5> \n <ul>\n  <li>IKEA <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/fixa-screwdriver-drill-lithium-ion-00196101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">FIXA Drill</a></li>\n  <li>Exterior/Interior furniture paint</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3Ck0M2r\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Acrylic paint pens</a></li>\n </ul> <h3>IKEA FALSTER garden set painted</h3> <p>Using the IKEA drill, I removed the slats from the chairs (seat area and handles) and the bench.</p> <p>Save all the screws.</p> <p>Cleaned and dried the slats and did a mild sanding.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"492\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-2.jpeg\" alt=\"garden bench\" class=\"wp-image-83676\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-2.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-2-550x264.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-2-768x369.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Painted the slats with the navy blue I picked up and using acrylic pens, I drew some designs on the chair handles. I did do two coats of the paint.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"736\" height=\"982\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-1_a.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA FALSTER garden set\" class=\"wp-image-83678\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-1_a.jpg 736w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-1_a-550x734.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 736px) 100vw, 736px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2019/09/ikea-outdoor-dining-table-restoration.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA outdoor dining table set gets real wood</a></li>\n </ul> <p>Let it dry for 24 hours and screw them back in.</p> <h5>What was the cost?</h5> <p>It cost me around $35. The expensive part was the <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3Ck0M2r\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">acrylic pens</a> I ordered on Amazon for $20. The paint was $9 from <a href=\"https://www.lowes.com/search?searchTerm=exterior%2Finterior+furniture+paint\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Lowes</a>. (They have a sale section near their paint department where they sell paints that are returned for $9/gallon) and rest of the money was spent on brushes.</p> <h5>What do you like most about the hack?</h5> <p>I really love that I was able to do a “Indian design” directly on the chairs.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-4.jpeg\" alt=\"IKEA FALSTER garden set\" class=\"wp-image-83677\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-4.jpeg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/falster-painted-4-550x733.jpeg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>What was the hardest part of the hack?</h5> <p>Not hard but definitely pay attention to make sure you covered each and every nook and corner to paint.</p> <h5>Anything to pay special attention to?</h5> <p>If I had to do this all over again, I would probably get some new set of nails on hand just in case.</p> <p>Also, I did not remove the slats from the dining table. I painted directly on the table.&nbsp;</p> <p>~ by SJ</p> </span>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/08/ikea-falster-garden-set.html\">IKEA FALSTER garden set itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>A candle that smells like meatballs? </p> <p>At the back of my head, I’m thinking this is a huge departure from the collaboration with Ben Gorham, which resulted in the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/new/osynlig-collection-13-scents-by-ikea-and-ben-gorham-pubab2cd080\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">OSYNLIG collection</a>, an artful range of 13 scents. </p> <p>But strangely this meatball candle got me more excited than Mr. Gorham’s concoctions.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-2.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HUVUDROLL meatball https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-2-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">\n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n    Photo: IKEA.com\n   </meta>\n  </meta></p> <p>IKEA created the HUVUDROLL Meatball Scented Candles to celebrate the 10 year anniversary of&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/ikea-family/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA Family</a>, the company’s loyalty programme. The goal is to bring the iconic smell from the store to your living room. Hmm … I’m not sure I want a lingering beefy scent in my home but TBH I’m curious whether it smells like the real thing. Aren’t you? </p> <p>“For many people,&nbsp;one of&nbsp;the first things&nbsp;that comes to mind when they think of IKEA is their delicious and affordable Swedish meatballs,” Sho Matsuzaki, creative director at Ogilvy, which spearheaded the creative project with IKEA, told <a href=\"https://nypost.com/2021/08/03/ikea-releases-meatball-scented-candles/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">The NY Post</a>. “There’s no other furniture brand out there with a food offering that has such a&nbsp;strong&nbsp;following. So for the IKEA Family 10-year anniversary, we thought it would be fitting to create something unexpected that our&nbsp;IKEA Family members and&nbsp;meatball&nbsp;super-fans&nbsp;would love. And yes, it does very much smell like IKEA meatballs.”</p> <h3>How to win the HUVUDROLL meatball scented candles</h3> <p>However, you can’t stroll into IKEA and buy a dozen of the unique beef-gravy-lingonberry candles. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HUVUDROLL meatball scented candles for IKEA FAMILY celebration\" class=\"wp-image-83696\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle.jpg 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> <p>To get your hands on them, you’ll need to be an IKEA Family member and register for the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/ikea-family/sweepstakes-pub76189570\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA Family 10th Anniversary Sweepstakes</a>. Be sure to log \n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   on to&nbsp;\n   <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/ikea-family/anniversary-pubabff5fc0\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA’s website</a>&nbsp;from August 6 to 22 to join the sweepstakes. No purchase is necessary, with the condition that members are 18+ and part of the U.S. IKEA Family Program.\n  </meta></p> <p>IKEA will select 986 participants as winners of an IKEA Prize Box which includes the limited edition HUVUDROLL Meatball candle and other items. The gift box promises to give winners an immersive sensory experience of being at an IKEA store. 1,925 Runner Up prize winners will each receive a \n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   HUVUDROLL candle. \n  </meta></p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-3.jpg\" alt=\"smells like ikea spirit\" class=\"wp-image-83697\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-3.jpg 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-3-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/ikea-limited-edition-huvudroll-meatball-scented-candle-3-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">\n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   Photo: IKEA.com\n  </meta></p> <p>It’s not the first time IKEA used their famous meatballs in a promotion. In April 2020 <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/04/ikea-meatball-recipe.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA released its signature recipe</a> with the cooking steps depicted in its usual assembly instruction drawings. </p> <p>Nor are they a stranger to experiences packed in a box. for holding up notes and photos. They work brilliantly for indoor plants, real or fake.</p> <p>Let’s take a leaf from IKEA hackers who have made IKEA memo boards work as an indoor plant trellis.</p> <h5>#1 Make it blend into the wall</h5> <p>Vesna hacked the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/korsmon-memo-board-with-clips-gold-20496288/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">KORSMON&nbsp;memo board</a> into an indoor wall plant trellis.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KORSMON.png\" alt=\"KORSMON memo board\" class=\"wp-image-83774\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KORSMON.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KORSMON-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KORSMON-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\"><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/korsmon-memo-board-with-clips-gold-20496288/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">KORSMON Memo board with clips</a> | IKEA.com</p> <p>All she needed was a spray of white paint. (You can also leave it in gold if you prefer it to stand out).</p> <p>Install it to the wall according to instructions. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"571\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/indoor-plant-trellis.jpg\" alt=\"indoor plant trellis hack\" class=\"wp-image-83772\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/indoor-plant-trellis.jpg 571w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/indoor-plant-trellis-550x616.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 571px) 100vw, 571px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>And tie your plant onto the frame with <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3xG0YoP\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">twist ties</a> or <a href=\"https://amzn.to/37DGwun\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">clips</a>. The memo board blends into the wall and the plant becomes the main focus.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"464\" height=\"639\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/indoor-plant-trellis-2.jpg\" alt=\"indoor plant trellis hack\" class=\"wp-image-83773\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/category/hacks/outdoor/plants\">Explore our page dedicated to IKEA hacks for plants</a></li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ul> <h5>#2 Spread it over a wall</h5> <p>Reddit user <a href=\"https://www.reddit.com/user/PlantTheEggplant/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PlantTheEggplant</a> opted for the black steel SÖSDALA memo board instead. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/SÖSDALA.png\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">SÖSDALA Memo board with clips</a> | IKEA.com</p> <p>The boards were installed in a 2 x 4 grid creating a living wall in the dining room.</p> \n <div plant pots</a>&nbsp;form an eye-catching feature. Keep them at a level where watering isn’t a pain. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/ikea-home-of-tomorow-8.jpg\" alt=\"\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>Your plants inching along slowly? Temporarily pad it up with <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/fejka-artificial-potted-plant-indoor-outdoor-hanging-40349531/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">FEKJA plants</a> while you cultivate your plants. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"340\" height=\"405\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/fekja-plants-trellis.png\" alt=\"indoor plant trellis hack\" class=\"wp-image-83778\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/ideas/increase-the-feeling-of-nature-with-plants-pub32022f01\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA.com</a></p> <p> </p> <h5>#3 Hang it over a sunny window</h5> <p>Hang the memo board over a window. It does not block the view and the plants get the light they need. Win-win.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"750\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KVICKSUND.png\" alt=\"KVICKSUND memo board\" class=\"wp-image-83776\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KVICKSUND.png 750w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KVICKSUND-550x367.png 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KVICKSUND-360x240.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\"><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/kvicksund-memo-board-white-30444958/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">KVICKSUND memo board</a> | IKEA.com</p> <p>Use string to hang up <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3m11v2r\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">propagation jars</a> and planters. And let them climb!</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/KVICKSUND-plant-trellis-1.jpg\" alt=\"indoor plant trellis hack\" class=\"wp-image-83779\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/jp/en/ideas/a-memo-board-for-multiple-use-recxsvpvgf7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA.com</a></p> <p></p> </span>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>After I adopted my two little doggies, I was looking for a place for them to sleep in my room where&nbsp;they were&nbsp;secure.&nbsp; Conventional crates were ugly and bulky.&nbsp; </p> <p>And then Covid hit, and I needed a desk where I could zoom with my students, so the limited floor space in my room needed to do double duty. </p> <p>Looking around online, showed only&nbsp;really expensive and heavy options for <a href=\"https://amzn.to/36UQRBL\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">dog crate&nbsp;desks</a>.&nbsp;</p> <h5>IKEA item used:</h5> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"500\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4.jpg\" alt=\"sniglar changing table\" class=\"wp-image-58680\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4.jpg 500w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4-50x50.jpg 50w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4-186x186.jpg 186w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> \n <ul>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/sniglar-changing-table-beech-white-50197589/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">SNIGLAR Changing Table</a>&nbsp; x 2</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/variera-plastic-bag-dispenser-white-80010222/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">VARIERA Plastic Bag Dispenser</a> x 8</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/lurvig-cushion-black-triangle-10463269/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">LURVIG Cushion&nbsp;</a>x 2</li>\n  <li>KLIMPEN table top&nbsp;</li>\n </ul> <h5>Other materials and tools:</h5> \n <ul>\n  <li>Drill</li>\n  <li>Scissors</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/36UpIyT\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">GooGone</a></li>\n  <li>Glue</li>\n  <li>Large White Zip Ties</li>\n  <li>Small floor protectors</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.homedepot.com/p/Lehigh-60-lb-x-3-9-16-in-Nickel-Plated-Steel-Double-End-Bolt-Snap-Hook-7004S-12/100114819\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Double Sided Snap Spring</a>&nbsp;x 2</li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.walmart.com/ip/5-PC-1-4-x-60mm-Carabiner-Spring-Snap-Hook-Marine-Stainless-Steel-140-Lbs/625724555\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Carabiner Spring Snap</a>&nbsp;x 2</li>\n </ul> <h3>Double dog crate + IKEA desk hack</h3> <p>1. Assemble the two SNIGLAR changing tables according to IKEA Instructions. </p> <p>2. Attach slider/gliders to the feet (optional).&nbsp; </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"767\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-3.jpg\" alt=\"double dog crates\" class=\"wp-image-83591\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-3.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-3-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-3-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2019/07/dog-cage-cover-decorative.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Dog cage cover that looks good and works even better</a></li>\n </ul> <p>3. After removing the sticky labels with <a href=\"https://amzn.to/36UpIyT\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">GooGone</a> (this was the most difficult and time consuming part of the hack),&nbsp; cut the VARIERA pieces to fit the sides of the SNIGLAR changing tables to create 3 fixed sides and one side that can open. </p> <p>For the “door” side, I used the natural “hinge” in the VARIERA and it worked well.&nbsp; For the longer sides, I used two of the large rectangle pieces and glued them together to form a long panel.&nbsp; </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"767\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-4.jpg\" alt=\"double dog crates\" class=\"wp-image-83592\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-4.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-4-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-4-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>4. Drill through the white bases on the changing table and the corresponding wood surrounds at 2-3 inch intervals around both the base and the top so that you can loop the zip ties through to secure the side panels to the changing table.&nbsp; </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"767\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-2.jpg\" alt=\"double dog crates with desk\" class=\"wp-image-83593\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-2.jpg 767w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-2-550x734.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 767px) 100vw, 767px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2018/07/dog-steps-diy-ikea-crates.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Small dog? DIY these dog steps from IKEA crates</a></li>\n </ul> <p>Make sure to have any sharp edges of the zip ties facing out so that your fur babies won’t contact them from the inside. </p> <p>5. Attach the carabiner&nbsp;and spring to the “door” and the “frame” so that you can secure the door in the closed position.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-gallery aligncenter columns-2 is-cropped\">\n  <ul class=\"blocks-gallery-grid\">\n   <li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\">\n    <figure>\n     <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6.jpg\" alt=\"carabiner\" data-id=\"83595\" data-full-url=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6.jpg\" data-link=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?attachment_id=83595\" class=\"wp-image-83595\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n    </figure></li>\n   <li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\">\n    <figure>\n     <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5.jpg\" alt=\"door\" data-id=\"83594\" data-full-url=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5.jpg\" data-link=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?attachment_id=83594\" class=\"wp-image-83594\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n    </figure></li>\n  </ul>\n </figure> <h5>How much did it cost and how long did it take?</h5> <p>This project was easily&nbsp;done over a&nbsp;weekend by one person,&nbsp;with the exception of lifting the heavy table top in place.&nbsp; The most time consuming piece was getting the stickers off of the plastic dispensers.&nbsp; But it was&nbsp;important that that side faced out so the inner side where the doggies sleep is smooth. The cost was around $150.00</p> <h5>What do you like most about the hack?</h5> <p>That the final product is easy and lightweight.&nbsp; The colors work in my room and it’s easy to dismantle if I wanted a change.&nbsp;</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate.jpg\" alt=\"double dog crates with desk\" class=\"wp-image-83597\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>I adjusted the opening where your legs go to be a bit bigger so I wouldn’t feel squeezed in.&nbsp; One nice bonus that I hadn’t anticipated is that the changing table ends act as little “trenches” where I can store lots of desk supplies without sacrificing my big desk surface.&nbsp;</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"767\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-1.jpg\" alt=\"double dog crates with desk\" class=\"wp-image-83596\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-1-550x412.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-1-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>What’s the hardest part of the Double Dog Crate Desk project?</h5> <p>The hardest part was figuring out what material to use for the crate sides.&nbsp; Once I stumbled on the VARIERA dispensers, it was easy because the dimensions work nearly perfectly with the openings, and they were easy enough to cut with good scissors along the seam lines.&nbsp;</p> <h5>What to pay special attention to?</h5> <p>I would pay attention to the size, weight, and temperament&nbsp;of your dogs to see if this would work for you.&nbsp; My guys are not chewers and are very calm (and only 15 pounds each), so they seem very secure and snug.&nbsp; They don’t push on the sides or try to get out. The build is solid but would likely not withstand a robust chewer.&nbsp;</p> <h5>Anything you would have done differently?</h5> <p>Looking back, I would consider adding casters to the bottom of the tables, but it was difficult finding ones that would fit the narrow legs of the SNIGLAR. I also did not attach the top to the bases, but it would likely be safer to do so.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> <p>~ by Alissa Davis</p> </span>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/07/double-dog-crate-desk.html\">Build your own Double Dog Crate with WFH Desk</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" +0000","feedId":65,"bgimg":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4.jpg","linkMd5":"f28a3e5f17dbd2662f802e41a220a7b6","destWidth":500,"destHeight":500,"sourceBytes":16358,"destBytes":9794,"author":"Contributor","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/sniglar-changing-table-white__0119722_PE276153_S4.jpg":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn56@2020_5/2021/08/15/03-55-01-639_180666cf0c15c62f.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-4.jpg":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn95@2020_5/2021/08/15/03-55-01-743_c44efdf38376402b.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-6.jpg":null,"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-5.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn12@2020_1/2021/08/15/03-55-02-009_630d98eee5975236.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn43@2020_5/2021/08/15/03-55-02-602_072d54d9065167be.webp","https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/double-dog-crate-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn20@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-01-727_c88835cb32fe73ad.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn32@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-02-316_05353866f732d1c2.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn72@2020_3/2021/08/15/03-55-01-886_1b4a6100740437d6.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/Ikeahacker?i=9r-o3cmILH8:Uj5iTLNGz8s:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn67@2020_1/2021/08/15/03-55-02-363_c65968910d170e92.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/Ikeahacker/~4/9r-o3cmILH8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn52@2020_6/2021/08/15/03-55-01-715_eeef911e15d0d777.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1628999639654},{"createdTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"10 ways to make plain IKEA PAX doors more attractive","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=83726","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p><strong>Question:</strong> I have 2 of these monstrosities in my front room. What funky ideas do you have for me to decorate the IKEA PAX doors so they put a smile on my face? </p> <p>How can I make these cupboards into something more attractive? </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-door-upgrade-1-rotated.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas\" class=\"wp-image-83727\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-door-upgrade-1-rotated.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-door-upgrade-1-550x733.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>~ by&nbsp;Susanne</p> \n <hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-dots\" /> <p>Hi Susanne</p> <p>Glad you asked. I had fun researching 10 ideas to turn the IKEA PAX wardrobe doors into a feature rather than a “monstrosity” as you call it. <img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/13.1.0/72x72/1f923.png\" alt=\"🤣\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /></p> <p>The ideas range from easy to more challenging ones. So, pick the idea that suits your style and skill level. That said, go ahead and attempt something fabulous. If you do screw up the doors, you can always pick up new ones at IKEA. </p> <p>I’ll start with the easy ones first.</p> <h5>#1 Change the hardware </h5> <p>One the simplest upgrade is to add a new set of door handles or knobs. Remove the plastic handles you have and go for statement handles. <a href=\"https://www.atelierabigailahern.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Abigail Ahern</a> made these with strips of wood, painted a hot pink. It’s not hard to <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XdyVUhZf62g\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">make a set</a> (if you have the tools) but you can also buy extra long wood handles like these on <a href=\"https://tidd.ly/2Ub0pG8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Etsy</a>. Leave them natural or spray paint if you prefer.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"475\" height=\"633\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/gemma7.jpeg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas\" class=\"wp-image-83728\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: Image by Graham Atkins Hughes via <a href=\"http://www.designsponge.com/2009/06/sneak-peek-gemma-ahren.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Design Sponge</a></p> <p>Not into long handles? <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3fOlhdG\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Brass pull rings</a> are pretty too. <br /></p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"682\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/brass-handles-1.jpeg\" alt=\"brass ring pulls\" class=\"wp-image-83729\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/brass-handles-1.jpeg 682w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/brass-handles-1-550x826.jpeg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 682px) 100vw, 682px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://andchristina.com/how-to-pax-wardrobe-hack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">AndChristina.com</a></p> <h5>#2 Adhesive wallpaper or contact paper</h5> <p>The days of messy wallpaper paste is over. <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/stores/page/DD09A695-8B4E-49B8-B1FB-3046DF3CDC02?ingress=2&amp;visitId=12c1faf9-65b5-4898-8488-dac93eb7332b&amp;ref_=ast_bln&amp;_encoding=UTF8&amp;tag=ikeahacker-20&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;linkId=630186aea93b8a5bd17efba068fd5872&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Peel and stick wallpaper</a> has transformed so many walls. It definitely will transform your PAX doors. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"684\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-pax-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas - wallpaper\" class=\"wp-image-83730\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-pax-1.jpg 684w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-pax-1-550x823.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 684px) 100vw, 684px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://www.seasonsincolour.com/post/2016-1-5-chic-ikea-hack-wardrobe-makeover\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Seasons In Colour</a></p> <p>Choose a design you like. Get as many rolls as needed. Thoroughly clean the surface of the PAX door and let it dry. Then cut out the wallpaper a little larger than the measurement of the PAX door. Stick from top edge and work your way down, pressing the paper firmly with a plastic card or squeegee. Lastly, cut off the excess edges with a <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3sd1oCg\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Xacto knife</a> or fold them onto the sides of the door. </p> <h5>#3 Make a fabric cover</h5> <p>This may be perfect for your front room. Depending on the fabric you choose you can totally turn it into an eye catching feature in the room. </p> <p>According to the tutorial in <a href=\"https://aroundthehouses.com/ikea-pax-wardrobe-hack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Around the House</a>, you’ll need fabric, sheets of MDF (<a href=\"https://amzn.to/3AsZSii\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">foam boards</a> may work too) and <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2VHbnnh\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Gorilla Glue</a>. Cut the MDF according to the size of the PAX doors, with an inch margin all round. Wrap the fabric around the MDF and glue the fabric down at the back of the boards. The final step is to glue the fabric panels on to the PAX doors. Make sure to use <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3fPCd3t\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">heavy duty construction adhesive</a>. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"825\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/fabric-pax-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas - fabric\" class=\"wp-image-83731\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/fabric-pax-1.jpg 825w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/fabric-pax-1-550x683.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/fabric-pax-1-768x953.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 825px) 100vw, 825px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://aroundthehouses.com/ikea-pax-wardrobe-hack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Around the Houses</a><br /></p> <h5>#4 Upgrade with mirror</h5> <p>This <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/10/domino-does-a-pax-hack.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">mirrored PAX door</a> would have been a walk in the park if you had <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/bergsbo-door-with-hinges-white-s29904178/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">BERGSBO doors</a>. You could have mirrors cut to the size of the squares and set them in place with adhesive. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/10/pax7.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas - mirrors\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\"><br>Photo: <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2013/10/domino-does-a-pax-hack.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Jenny Komenda via Domino</a></br></p> <p>To recreate a similar look on flat PAX doors, I would suggest <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/lots-mirror-40507262/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">LOTS mirrors</a>. Stick the mirrors onto the door and finish with a strip of wood trim around the mirrors. Painting the doors and trim first would be great too.</p> <h5>#5 Cane weave on doors</h5> <p>If mirrors aren’t your thing, how about <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3s6QFcc\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">cane webbing</a>? Or even <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3lPbw2U\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">burlap</a> for a rustic, natural look.</p> \n <blockquote class=\"instagram-media\" font-weight:normal; line-height:17px; text-decoration:none;\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">A post shared by Fronteriors (@fronteriors)</a></p>\n  </div>\n </blockquote> <script async=\"\" src=\"//www.instagram.com/embed.js\"></script> <h5>#6 Add texture</h5> <p>A padded wardrobe door can look and feel luxurious. An easy way to do it would be to use <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3m2WDu3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">embossed panels</a> <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2Vyk0AR\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">like this</a>. Besides padding, you can try <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3s6fsNV\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">acoustics foam panels</a>. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1.jpeg\" alt=\"padded\" class=\"wp-image-83733\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1.jpeg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1-550x550.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1-150x150.jpeg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1-768x768.jpeg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/pax-padded-1-125x125.jpeg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\"><br>Photo: <a href=\"https://www.apartmenttherapy.com/ikea-hacks-10-diy-ways-to-make-cheap-wardrobes-look-more-expensive-202389\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Apartment Therapy</a></br></p> <h5> #7 Add trim</h5> <p>If you like the vintage vibe, <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/02/victorian-home-wardrobe.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">this hack</a> is perfect for your two PAX wardrobes. Kevin and Sarah turned theirs into a built-in with lots of delightful touches. Such as the trim on the doors which elevates the stock IKEA PAX doors into awesomeness. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/02/victorian-home-wardrobe.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See the hack here</a>.<br /></p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/After-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas - trim\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h5>#8 Farmhouse style</h5> <p>If you are good at calculating angles, then try this criss-cross farmhouse style doors on for size. You’ll need thin strips of plywood and a <a href=\"https://amzn.to/2VISFvJ\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">table saw</a>, at the very least, to hack this. <a href=\"https://blog.jennasuedesign.com/2014/06/master-makeover-ikea-pax-door-hack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See her tutorial</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650\" height=\"975\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/PAX-farmhouse-door.jpeg\" alt=\"farmhouse style wardrobe\" class=\"wp-image-83732\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/PAX-farmhouse-door.jpeg 650w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/PAX-farmhouse-door-550x825.jpeg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 650px) 100vw, 650px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: <a href=\"https://blog.jennasuedesign.com/2014/06/master-makeover-ikea-pax-door-hack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Jenna Sue Design</a></p> <h5>#9 Chevron doors</h5> <p>Technically, this <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/06/chevron-doors-ikea-platsa.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">chevron design is on a PLATSA door</a> but I don’t see why it wouldn’t apply to your PAX doors. Steph and James ripped MDF into strips and then used a mitre saw to cut the 45 degree angles. They glued the strips on the doors and finished them with paint. <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2021/06/chevron-doors-ikea-platsa.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">See the tutorial</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/06/platsa-chevron-doors-1.jpg\" alt=\"chevron doors\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>You can tailor the design to your taste. Instead of chevrons, you can have them shiplap style, as diamonds or squares. Have fun designing it. </p> <h5>#10 Paint a mural</h5> <p>On my list this is definitely the hardest, because I can’t draw to save my life. Stacey painstaking <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2016/06/pax-mural.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">reproduced the mural on the doors</a> by hand. Not for the faint hearted. However, there are easier ways to do this. <a href=\"https://vintagerevivals.com/bathroom-reveal-paint-by-numbers-wall-mural/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Vintage Revivals</a> has a superb tutorial on transforming a mural design into a paint-by-numbers kind of art. Very cool. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/05/pax-mural_3.jpeg\" alt=\"IKEA PAX doors ideas - mural\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>So, \n  <meta charset=\"utf-8\">\n   Susanne, which is your favourite way to hack your IKEA PAX doors? Let us know and \n   <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/submit-hack\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">share your finished project with us</a>.\n  </meta></p> <p>Happy hacking,</p> </ul> <h3>IKEA RABBLA Space Divider</h3> <p>The RABBLA storage box comes with dividers that create 4 basic compartments. Each compartment may still be too large for smaller items you wish to store. </p> <p>The first thing you might feel the need is to divide the 4 basic compartments into smaller customized dimensions. So we start the customization with a simple divider. The divider has 2 parts: the main divider and the ender for reasons you’ll soon understand. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4808185\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Link to STL files</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-gallery columns-2 is-cropped\">\n  <ul class=\"blocks-gallery-grid\">\n   <li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\">\n    <figure>\n     <img loading=\"lazy\"
