small objects. This is the first of a series of solutions for this need. It replaces the main part of the Space Divider and combines with the ender. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4830921\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA RABBLA box with compartments with pocket\" class=\"wp-image-83609\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/space_divider_with_pocket_detail-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h3>IKEA RABBLA Rack Space Divider</h3> <p>As a maker I have many small tools such as pliers and screwdrivers. A rack helps to keep them in view and ready to use, so I created this rack (it works best in pairs!) It can also be useful, for example, to keep in order brushes and cutters for painting and modeling enthusiasts. Like the previous item, it replaces the main divider and integrates with the ender. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4853531\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail.jpg\" alt=\"rack\" class=\"wp-image-83610\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/rack_space_divider_detail-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/10/3d-printed-add-ons.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Designer improves on IKEA with 6 thoughtful hacks</a></li>\n </ul> <h3>Ender with Pocket</h3> <p>If the standard ender is not enough, this version, compatible with all previous dividers integrates a pocket. Very useful as a pen holder. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4876412\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail.jpg\" alt=\"pocket for small items\" class=\"wp-image-83611\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ender_with_pocket_detail-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h3>Small Items Tray</h3> <p>Small objects can be difficult to find quickly if scattered around the large container. So I designed this tray. It hangs on the central frame or on the simple divider, so you can easily reach for the small objects. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4676886\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\">\n  <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/small_items_tray-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n </figure> <h3>Hanging Pocket</h3> <p>Similar to the previous one, with the same positioning possibilities, this pocket is designed for slightly larger objects, such as a power bank or hand sanitizer. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4658794\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\">\n  <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/hanged_pocket.jpg\" alt=\"for larger objects\" class=\"wp-image-83613\" Printer framework never looked so good</a></li>\n </ul> <h3>Multilevel Small Items Container</h3> <p>Especially dedicated to small objects I made this accessory which allows you to store them clearly in view on 3 small tiers. The space underneath remains free, letting you store markers or similar items in the compartment. Also it can be used independently. To hang it on the RABBLA use the dedicated hook. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4759200\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\">\n  <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA RABBLA box with compartments with multi tier storage\" class=\"wp-image-83614\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray-768x768.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/multilevel_small_items_tray-125x125.jpg 125w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n </figure> <h3>WhiteBoard Lid Adapter</h3> <p>Last but not least, I present one last accessory. This one needs a bit of extra DIY in addition to printing the STL. The adapter allows you to hook the lid to the frame and prop up the lid to use as a whiteboard. You’ll also need to glue an A4 laminated sheet, with a hole cut in the center, to the lid. <a href=\"https://www.thingiverse.com/thing:4630818\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get the file</a>.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-gallery columns-2 is-cropped\">\n  <ul class=\"blocks-gallery-grid\">\n   <li class=\"blocks-gallery-item\">\n    <figure>\n     <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/whiteboard_lid_adapter_detail.jpg\" alt=\"ikea rabbla whiteboard lid adapter\" data-id=\"83615\" data-full-url=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/whiteboard_lid_adapter_detail.jpg\" data-link=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?attachment_id=83615\" class=\"wp-image-83615\" https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/whiteboard_lid_adapter_detail-550x550.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/whiteboard_lid_adapter_detail-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/whiteboard_lid_adapter_detail-768x768.jpg 768w, convert the lid to a whiteboard:<br>1. Laminate a white sheet of A4 sized paper.<br>2. Stick it on the lid using double-sided tape.<br>3. Recreate the hole in the lid using a cutter.<br>4. Fit the 3D printed adapter onto the cover and the frame as shown in the photo<br>5. Write using the <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3eYbNMs\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">special markers for whiteboards</a>.</br></br></br></br></br></p> <p>Have fun with your personalized IKEA RABBLA! </p> <p>I hope that the community of <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net\">IkeaHackers</a> and <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/category/hacks/3d\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/ivar\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IVAR</a> shelving unit for nursery storage and I’ve bought a hanging rail from the system to make a ‘wardrobe’ for my daughter’s clothes. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"853\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-kids-room-1-1.jpeg\" alt=\"ikea ivar kids wardrobe\" class=\"wp-image-83644\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-kids-room-1-1.jpeg 853w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-kids-room-1-1-550x660.jpeg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-kids-room-1-1-768x922.jpeg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 853px) 100vw, 853px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>The plan was to add <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/gb/en/p/ivar-door-10453072/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">these doors</a>&nbsp;to help stop the sun fading the clothes, which would have worked perfectly. As far as I can tell, they would not have required me to drill any extra holes in the shelves. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"483\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-cane-door-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA bamboo weave door\" class=\"wp-image-83639\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-cane-door-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-cane-door-1-550x259.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-cane-door-1-768x362.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> <p>Sadly I was not quick enough and they’re now almost completely sold out online and across the UK.</p> <p>I’ve seen lots of <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?s=ivar+cabinet\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IVAR cabinet door hacks</a> but not so much for the shelving. Can anyone advise?!</p> <p>Thank you!</p> <p>~ by Becki </p> \n <hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-dots\" /> <p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Hi Becki</p> <p>Ah … that’s frustrating. There aren’t many door options for the IVAR and the cane webbing doors get snapped up the moment they restock. I can hardly get hold of them at my local IKEA either. </p> <p>Firstly, the bamboo weave doors you want may still be available on eBay, Amazon or FB Marketplace. I did a search and <a href=\"https://www.ebay.co.uk/itm/224550643140?hash=item344842e5c4:g:518AAOSw1ilhAX~a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">found this one</a>.</p> <p>As for alternatives for the IVAR door, you are right. I’ve not seen many door hacks for the IVAR shelving unit.</p> <p>So here is what I came up with. </p> <h5>#1 DIY IVAR door alternatives</h5> <p>You can make your own doors for IVAR. Hester has a <a href=\"https://www.hestershandmadehome.com/hestershandmadehome/ikeaivarhack\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">wonderful tutorial</a> for DIY IVAR doors which can be so interesting for a kid’s wardrobe. </p> <p>She measured the space and got the plywood cut to size at the hardware store. Then, attached them to the IVAR side units with <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3f9IC9n\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">hinges</a>. She finished them with <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/search/ref=as_li_qf_sp_sr_il_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=ikeahacker-20&amp;keywords=peel and stick wallpaper&amp;index=aps&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;linkId=c271476664feaf2f4b04229a94b76a9a\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">peel and stick wallpaper</a> to personalise the doors. I’m sure your creative juices are pumping now.</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\">\n  <div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\"> \n   <iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"Ikea Ivar Hack,  bookcase into a stylish cabinet\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/cyx8tAlSuF4?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe> \n  </div>\n </figure> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related</strong>: <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/02/kids-room-decorating-ideas.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">20 fabulous kids room decorating ideas from this Instagram Hashtag</a></li>\n </ul> <p>She has another version using reclaimed doors. Very cool too, with hinges on display. </p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\">\n  <div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\"> \n   <iframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"Ikea Ivar hack wardrobe build with reclaimed doors, part 2\" width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/6gh5_JpXJLA?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe> \n  </div>\n </figure> <p>You could try plywood, pine or any wood planks too. </p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n   <img src=\"https://ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/ivar.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA IVAR door alternatives \" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>See this <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2015/08/diy-tall-ivar-wardrobe.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">wardrobe for long jackets and coats from IVAR</a>.</p> <h5>#2 Fabric covers</h5> <p>IKEA used to sell fabric covers for the IVAR system. You may still be able to find them on online marketplaces.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"576\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-fabric-cover-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA IVAR door alternatives - fabric cover\" class=\"wp-image-83637\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-fabric-cover-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-fabric-cover-1-550x309.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/ivar-fabric-cover-1-768x432.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> <p>Alternatively, you can use blinds like the <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/gb/en/p/sandvedel-roller-blind-beige-60467199/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">80 cm wide SANDVEDEL</a> or <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/gb/en/p/ringblomma-roman-blind-white-90258062/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">RINGBLOMMA</a> to cover up the front of the IVAR. Add a plank across the top shelf and then attach the blind to it. </p> <h5>#3 Picture frame door</h5> <p>One final idea to consider for your alternative IVAR door. Picture frames!</p> \n <figure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\">\n  <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"380\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/hovsta-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA IVAR door alternatives - picture frame\" class=\"wp-image-83638\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/hovsta-1.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/hovsta-1-550x204.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/07/hovsta-1-768x285.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n </figure> <p class=\"has-text-align-center has-small-font-size\">Photo: IKEA.com</p> <p>The <a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/gb/en/p/hovsta-frame-birch-effect-20365744/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">HOVSTA picture frame (40cmx50cm)</a> is as wide as one of the IKEA IVAR cane doors (42cm) so it might just work. Screw on hinges (or use strong adhesive) to the sides of the photo frame and then attach to the side units. You can use shorter frames too if your shelves are closer together. What I love about this idea is how useful the frames can be. You can use the picture frames to label what’s behind the doors. Or to display your child’s artwork or family photos. So fun! This <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2015/01/gladsax-frames-doors-kallax-expedit.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">tutorial</a> may be helpful. </p> <p>Hope you’re inspired to do something different for your kid’s wardrobe. Do share your IVAR door alternatives with us.</p> <p>Happy hacking,</p> <p>Jules</p> \n <hr class=\"wp-block-separator is-style-default\" /> <p class=\"has-text-align-center\"><em>Hacking may compromise the structural integrity of the item, so please be aware of the risks involved before modifying or altering any IKEA product. 11:53:59","updatedTime":"2021-08-15 11:53:59","title":"IKEA HEMNES dresser refreshed with tropical wallpaper","link":"https://www.ikeahackers.net/?p=83712","description":"<span class=\"cb-itemprop\" itemprop=\"reviewBody\"> <p>A rather tired and old looking IKEA Hemnes dresser was given a fresh tropical makeover with wallpaper.</p> <h5>IKEA product:&nbsp; </h5> \n <ul>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.ikea.com/us/en/p/hemnes-3-drawer-chest-black-brown-90360413/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">IKEA Hemnes large drawers</a></li>\n </ul> <h5>Other Products used:&nbsp;&nbsp;</h5> \n <ul>\n  <li><a href=\"https://www.anniesloan.com/product/chalk-paint/oxford-navy/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Chalk paint in Oxford Navy</a></li>\n  <li>Affordable tropical wallpaper – <a href=\"https://amzn.to/37r3Dbh\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">bought off Amazon</a></li>\n  <li><a href=\"https://amzn.to/3AnHC9V\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">Wallpaper paste</a></li>\n  <li>New large round wooden knobs<br /></li>\n </ul> <p>My neighbour threw out an old IKEA <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/tag/hemnes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">HEMNES</a> chest of drawers. I decided to rescue the piece and give it a fresh update.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> <h3>Here’s how it was before.</h3> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"682\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/Dresser-before-1.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES chest of drawers\" class=\"wp-image-83713\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/Dresser-before-1.jpg 682w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/Dresser-before-1-550x826.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 682px) 100vw, 682px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <h3>How to makeover the HEMNES dresser with wallpaper</h3> <p>1.&nbsp;First, I wiped down the whole piece to remove any dirt and dust.</p> <p>2. Next, I removed the drawers and gave the frame a&nbsp;fresh coat of chalk paint in Oxford Navy.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"682\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-the-dresser-3.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES dresser makeover with wallpaper and paint\" class=\"wp-image-83714\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-the-dresser-3.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-the-dresser-3-550x366.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-the-dresser-3-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-the-dresser-3-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>3. When the paint dried, I&nbsp;coated the frame with a layer of <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3iwOZpl\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener nofollow\">furniture wax</a> to protect it.</p> <p>4. Next, I painted the new wooden knobs for the drawers with the same chalk paint.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"682\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-knob-blue-4.jpg\" alt=\"wooden knobs\" class=\"wp-image-83716\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-knob-blue-4.jpg 682w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/painting-knob-blue-4-550x826.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 682px) 100vw, 682px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2020/06/hemnes-dresser-hack-3.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Glam HEMNES Dresser Hack. No power tools needed.</a></li>\n </ul> <p>5. Next, the drawer fronts. They weren’t painted but covered in gorgeous tropical print wallpaper. I took extra care to make sure&nbsp;that the patterned print on the wallpaper matched across all three of the drawer fronts.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"682\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wrapping-paper-round-door-6.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES dresser makeover with wallpaper and paint\" class=\"wp-image-83715\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wrapping-paper-round-door-6.jpg 682w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wrapping-paper-round-door-6-550x826.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 682px) 100vw, 682px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>6.&nbsp; To finish, I added new knobs to the drawer fronts.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1024\" height=\"682\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-drawers-ft-5.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES dresser makeover with wallpaper and paint\" class=\"wp-image-83718\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-drawers-ft-5.jpg 1024w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-drawers-ft-5-550x366.jpg 550w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-drawers-ft-5-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/wallpaper-drawers-ft-5-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> <p>I love how bright and fun the updated chest of drawers look now.&nbsp; It is certainly a statement piece.&nbsp; Now the neighbours have seen what we did with their old piece of IKEA furniture, they want it back!</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n   <img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"682\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/finished-IKEA-hemnes-hack-closeup-2.jpg\" alt=\"IKEA HEMNES dresser makeover with wallpaper and paint\" class=\"wp-image-83717\" srcset=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/finished-IKEA-hemnes-hack-closeup-2.jpg 682w, https://www.ikeahackers.net/wp-content/uploads/2021/08/finished-IKEA-hemnes-hack-closeup-2-550x826.jpg 550w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 682px) 100vw, 682px\" />\n  </figure>\n </div> \n <ul class=\"has-luminous-vivid-orange-color has-text-color\">\n  <li><strong>Related: </strong><a href=\"https://www.ikeahackers.net/2017/03/hemnes-karlby-kitchen-island-storage-seating.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">IKEA HEMNES hacked into a Kitchen Island with Seating and Storage</a></li>\n </ul> <p>This was a very affordable IKEA hack. I needed only a small amount of chalk paint for the frame and the wallpaper only cost about $20 for the whole roll.&nbsp; There is plenty of paper left over for matching furniture upcycles.</p> <p>See the full tutorial of the <a href=\"https://www.pillarboxblue.com/ikea-hemnes-hack-upcycled-drawers-with-wallpaper/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">HEMNES makeover</a> on my blog.</p>
